. gen close350not2500 = .

. replace close350not2500 = 0 if t_closeness_2 == 1
(8,402 real changes made)

.

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

    Ha: diff < 0                 Ha: diff != 0                 Ha: diff > 0
 Pr(Z < z) = 0.1066         Pr(|Z| > |z|) = 0.2133          Pr(Z > z) = 0.8934

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. 
. qui logit voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust iter(500)

. local loglik: display %8.3f `e(ll)'

. local pr2: display %4.3f `e(r2_p)'

.   local warning = "Convergence Not Achieved!"

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. 
. qui logit voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust iter(500)

. local modelname = "State = Minnesota"

. include Closeness_SubProgramPRTestRegression.do

. prtest voted_2014_primary `modelrestriction', by(close350not2500)

Two-sample test of proportions                     0: Number of obs =     2372
                                                   1: Number of obs =     2295
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    Variable |       Mean   Std. Err.      z    P>|z|     [95% Conf. Interval]
-------------+----------------------------------------------------------------
           0 |   .1648398   .0076183                      .1499082    .1797714
           1 |   .1782135   .0079884                      .1625566    .1938704
-------------+----------------------------------------------------------------
        diff |  -.0133737   .0110387                     -.0350092    .0082617
             |  under Ho:   .0110348    -1.21   0.226
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        diff = prop(0) - prop(1)                                  z =  -1.2120
    Ho: diff = 0

    Ha: diff < 0                 Ha: diff != 0                 Ha: diff > 0
 Pr(Z < z) = 0.1128         Pr(|Z| > |z|) = 0.2255          Pr(Z > z) = 0.8872

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. 
. qui logit voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust iter(500)

. local loglik: display %8.3f `e(ll)'

. local pr2: display %4.3f `e(r2_p)'

. if `e(ic)' == 500 {
.   local warning = "Convergence Not Achieved!"
. }

. else {
.   local warning = " "
. }

. 
. putexcel A`row' = "`modelname'" B`row' = "`prop350'" C`row' = "`prop2500'" D`row' = "`diffprop' [`diffpropse']" E`row' = "`coef' [`se']" F`row' 
> = "(`n350',`n2500')"

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. local modelname = "State = Tennessee"

Two-sample test of proportions                     0: Number of obs =      636
                                                   1: Number of obs =      653
------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    Variable |       Mean   Std. Err.      z    P>|z|     [95% Conf. Interval]
-------------+----------------------------------------------------------------
           0 |    .413522   .0195275                      .3752488    .4517952
           1 |   .4287902   .0193671                      .3908315    .4667489

        diff |  -.0152682   .0275028                     -.0691728    .0386364
             |  under Ho:   .0275079    -0.56   0.579

        diff = prop(0) - prop(1)                                  z =  -0.5550
    Ho: diff = 0

    Ha: diff < 0                 Ha: diff != 0                 Ha: diff > 0
 Pr(Z < z) = 0.2894         Pr(|Z| > |z|) = 0.5789          Pr(Z > z) = 0.7106

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. 
. qui logit voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust iter(500)

. local loglik: display %8.3f `e(ll)'

. local pr2: display %4.3f `e(r2_p)'

. if `e(ic)' == 500 {
.   local warning = "Convergence Not Achieved!"
. }

. else {
.   local warning = " "
. }

. 
. putexcel A`row' = "`modelname'" B`row' = "`prop350'" C`row' = "`prop2500'" D`row' = "`diffprop' [`diffpropse']" E`row' = "`coef' [`se']" F`row' 
> = "(`n350',`n2500')"

. local ++row

. 
. local modelname = "State = Wisconsin"

. local modelrestriction = `"if vf_state == "WI""'

. include Closeness_SubProgramPRTestRegression.do

. 
. prtest voted_2014_primary `modelrestriction', by(close350not2500)

    Variable |       Mean   Std. Err.      z    P>|z|     [95% Conf. Interval]

        diff = prop(0) - prop(1)                                  z =  -0.5341
    Ho: diff = 0

    Ha: diff < 0                 Ha: diff != 0                 Ha: diff > 0
 Pr(Z < z) = 0.2966         Pr(|Z| > |z|) = 0.5933          Pr(Z > z) = 0.7034

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. 
. qui logit voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust iter(500)

. local loglik: display %8.3f `e(ll)'

. local pr2: display %4.3f `e(r2_p)'

. if `e(ic)' == 500 {
.   local warning = "Convergence Not Achieved!"
. }

. else {
.   local warning = " "
. }

> = "(`n350',`n2500')"

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. local modelname = "Either House Primary Competitive"

. include Closeness_SubProgramPRTestRegression.do

. prtest voted_2014_primary `modelrestriction', by(close350not2500)

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. 
. qui logit voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust iter(500)

. local loglik: display %8.3f `e(ll)'

. local pr2: display %4.3f `e(r2_p)'

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. 
. qui reg voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust

. local coef: display %4.3f _b[close350not2500]

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]

. 
. qui logit voted_2014_primary close350not2500 i.strata Z_* `modelrestriction' [pweight = weight_allstatestreats], robust iter(500)

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. local prop350: display %4.3f `r(P_2)'

. local prop2500: display %4.3f `r(P_1)'

. local diffproptemp = `r(P_2)'-`r(P_1)'

. local diffprop: display %4.3f `diffproptemp'

. local diffpropsetemp = sqrt(((`r(P_1)' * (1 - `r(P_1)')) / `r(N_1)') + ((`r(P_2)' * (1 - `r(P_2)')) / `r(N_2)'))

. local diffpropse: display %4.3f `diffpropsetemp'

. local n350 `r(N_2)'

. local n2500 `r(N_1)'

. local se: display %4.3f _se[close350not2500]
